In ÅšrÄ«mad-BhÄgavatam (10.29.15) it is stated that if one approaches the Supreme Lord even out of lust, anger or fear (kÄmaá¹ krodhaá¹ bhayam), he is purified. The gopÄ«s, being young girls, approached Ká¹›á¹£á¹‡a because He was a beautiful young boy. From the external point of view, they approached the Lord out of lust, and the Lord danced with them at midnight. ÅšrÄ« Caitanya MahÄprabhu therefore never publicly discussed Ká¹›á¹£á¹‡aâ€™s dealings with the gopÄ«s. He used to discuss these dealings only with three confidential friends.
